When checking into the room, I pressed the room number written by the front desk, but I couldn‚Äôt find the room after going around. I had to ask the staff who was cleaning the room for help, and then found that the front desk had written a room number that didn‚Äôt exist.

The river view king bed room is spacious, bright, and well-equipped. The roller blind is an automatic induction type, and it will automatically rise when entering the room. I like the desk facing the big window, and it is also enjoyable to work facing the night view at night. There are free drinks and snacks in the minibar, as well as two free bottles of Foss water. The bedding and toiletries are not bad, but I don‚Äôt understand why the trash can next to the toilet in the bathroom is stepped on. You have to pull the trash can to your feet and step on it to throw toilet paper.

Because I wanted to taste the market breakfast in Nanjing, I didn‚Äôt book a hotel breakfast when I booked a river view king bed room. It happened that I woke up very early on Saturday. After packing my luggage, I went out to eat the famous Liji beef pot stickers. I called the guests at 7:30 because they thought the guests would not get up. Could it be that the front desk staff who work in the morning thought that the guests would wake up when they went to work? The room that I said yesterday could not be tidied up early, and the hotel staff can carry the luggage. After communicating with the housekeeper, the hotel personnel moved the luggage to the suite.

In the evening, I went back to the hotel to stay in a suite. The room was rectangular, with a small living room on the outside, a toilet-washbasin-shower room in the middle, and a bedroom at the end. There was a long corridor on one side, and a bay window and a bathtub on the other side. In this way, the suite, which was originally small in size, became a dojo in a screw shell, and the space was even more cramped than the river-view king-bed room I stayed in the night before. The automatic curtains in the living room can be raised automatically when entering the door, but they cannot be lowered automatically, and the switch is behind the wide sofa. To close the curtains, you have to step on the sofa to adjust it, which is a bit laborious.

Suite includes buffet breakfast. Freshly cut ham is the selling point, but the highlight is the freshly fried fritters, which are crispy and crispy. They are the most market-like fritters I have ever eaten in a five-star hotel, but I don‚Äôt know how the hotel‚Äôs food and beverage management staff handle other details. The place where the salad is served is not a slightly larger plate, but a saucer that is about the size of a saucer, and there is no way to put much salad. Hot soy milk and hot milk are heated on the induction cooker in the enamel pot, but there is a bowl next to it. There is no cup. It is normal to drink salty soy milk with a bowl, but it is used to drink hot milk. This is the boldness of Andaz? Is it because the hotel wants guests to taste the authentic skin belly noodles? Well, at least the noodles can be less, otherwise there is really no appetite for a bowl full of noodles without any soup.

The hotel is located in the new financial circle. There are not many supporting facilities around. It is a bit far away from major scenic spots. You need to take a taxi.
